 akshay tritiya kaa hindu dharma main khaas mahatv he
 It is also called Akha Teej
 har saal baishakh maas ke shukla paksh kii tritiya ko akshay tritiya kaha jaataa he
 This time Akshaya Tritiya is on 18 April and on this day you can do many auspicious tasks
 is baar suryoday purv se lekar raatri main 3:03 baje tak akshay tritiya rahegi
 Although it is said that the third of the Shukla Paksha of every month is auspicious, but Akshaya Tritiya has special significance
 akshay kaa shabdic arth he jiskaa kabhi kshay naa ho arthath jo sthai bana rahe
 It can remain permanent which is always true
 yah baaten nishchit rup se kahi ja sakati he ki satya keval paramatma hi he jo akshay, akhand or vyapak he
 This Akshaya Tritiya Tithi is Ishwar Tithi
 yah akshay tithi parashuram ji kaa janmdin hone ke kaaran parashuram tithi bhi kahi jaati he
 This day is auspicious coincidence of planets - On this day a special combination of planets is made
 - surya or chandramaa apni ucch raashi main hote he
 - This happens only once a year
 - surya, mesh main hota he or chandramaa vrishabh main hota he
 In the scriptures, the Sun has been considered our soul and the Moon as our mind
 - surya or chandramaa kaa sambandh banane kii vajah se ye tithi bahut mahatvapurn ho jaati he
 Therefore, whatever work is done on this day, its fruit will be doubled and will never end

 - On this day, wearing new clothes, jewelry and inauguration of new organization and work is considered auspicious
 - puranic manyata he ki is din pitru paksh ko kiya gaya tarpan or pindadaan yaa kisi bhi tarah kaa daan akshay fal detaa he
 Ganga bath and worship performed on this day destroys all sins
 baishakh ke maheene main khub khaaen kharbooza, or daan bhi karen- sampannataa kii kaamana har insaan ko hoti he
 For this reason, buying gold on this day will mean that Akshay will never end
 - akshay tritiya ko kiya gaya jap, tap, havan, puja, daan kaa fal kai guna bad jaataa he
 - On this day, we should pray for virtues and apologize for sins committed unknowingly

 Resumes are the first step to get a job
 isamen galati karne par yaa ghisi-pity chizon ko likhane kaa matlab hota he ki aapako naukari milane main deree ho sakati he
 At the same time, another problem is mostly with resumes that she is always full of old information
 hamamen se zyaadaatar log ek baar rigeume banaate hai or use samay-samay par apadet karnaa jaruri nahin samajhate hai
 Know that these changes should happen in your resume from time to time
 
 
 1
 It is important to give details of the recent work done: Before hiring a recruiter, they want to know about the candidate, how it will be beneficial for their company
 How will the company get the position on which the candidate is working in a company after he has benefited? Not only this, they also see how long the candidate has been carrying out his responsibilities
 isliye kuch bhi nayaa karen to use rigeume main apadet karnaa naa bhoolen
 2
 rigeume kaa kiwards:ctrl+f kaa upyog recruiters aapke rigeume dekhne ke liye karte hai
 There are many keywords that they can search in your resume
 samay ke anusaar aapkaa rigeume chalane vaala he yaa nahin iskaa pataa rigeume main istemaal kiye gaye kiwards se chalata he
 Some important words are necessary to grab the attention of the rootwriters, so place these words in the r√©sum√© as well
 3
 Remove essential personal details from resumes: In some r√©sum√©s, family states, citizenship, weight and height are written
 behatar yah hoga ki in sari jaankariyon ko aap khud tak rakhen
 You will not get any benefit by writing these things in the resume
 agar apkerizumemen ye jaankariyaan hai to use aaj hi apadet kar len
